              <div class=" cws-content-block ">
                <div class="cws-content-block__content ">
                  <div
                    class="cws-body text-block-module__description cws-content-block__text">
                    <p>Effective Date: January 18, 2024</p>
                    <p>This Google Cloud Privacy Notice describes how we collect
                      and process your personal information in relation
                      to&nbsp;<a href="https://workspace.google.com/intl/en/terms/user_features.html" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="google workspace including google workspace for education" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="workspace.google.com/intl/en/terms/user_features.html" track-metadata-module="text blocks">Google Workspace (including Google Workspace for Education)</a>,&nbsp;<a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/services" class="cws-link" track-name="google cloud platform" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/services">Google Cloud Platform</a>,
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/marketplace/launcher" class="cws-link" track-name="google cloud marketplace" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/marketplace/launcher">Google Cloud Marketplace</a>,
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/identity/user-features.html" class="cws-link" track-name="cloud identity" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/identity/user-features.html">Cloud Identity</a>
                      (when sold separately) and
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/professional-services" class="cws-link" track-name="implementation services" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/professional-services">Implementation Services</a>
                      (together, “Cloud Services”).</p>
                    <p>We offer Cloud Services to our customers either directly
                      or via our authorized partners. Where we refer to our
                      customers in this notice, we also mean our partners and
                      their customers.</p>
                    <p>If European Union (EU), UK or Swiss data protection law
                      applies to the processing of Service Data relating to you,
                      you can review the
                      ‘<a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-9" class="cws-link" track-name="european privacy standards and gdpr" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">European Privacy Standards and GDPR</a>’
                      section below to learn more about your rights and Google’s
                      compliance with these laws.</p>
                    <p>If your organization has entered into our
                      <a href="https://workspace.google.com/terms/service-data-addendum.html" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="google workspace for education service data addendum" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="workspace.google.com/terms/service-data-addendum.html">Google Workspace for Education Service Data Addendum</a>,
                      please review the
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice-supplement" class="cws-link" track-name="supplemental google cloud privacy notice" track-type="content block" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice-supplement">Supplemental Google Cloud Privacy Notice</a>
                      together with this notice.</p>
                    <p></p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div class="text-block-module__collapse-items cws-spacer-4--bottom">
              <cws-accordion expand-all="">
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-1"
                  panel-title="Service Data We Collect">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>Google processes Customer Data, Partner Data and Service
                      Data to provide Cloud Services. This Privacy Notice
                      applies solely to Service Data and <strong>does
                        not</strong> apply to Customer Data or Partner Data. We
                      explain what we mean by “Service Data” below.</p>
                    <p>Customer Data and Partner Data are defined in the
                      agreement(s) with our customers covering Cloud Services
                      and represent the data that you and our customers provide
                      for processing in Cloud Services. For more information
                      about how we process Customer Data and Partner Data, see
                      our
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/data-processing-addendum/" class="cws-link" track-name="cloud data processing addendum customers" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/data-processing-addendum/" track-metadata-module="text blocks">Cloud Data Processing Addendum (Customers)</a>
                      and
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/data-processing-terms/partner" class="cws-link" track-name="cloud data processing addendum partners" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/data-processing-terms/partner">Cloud Data Processing Addendum (Partners)</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p>Service Data is the personal information Google collects
                      or generates during the provision and administration of
                      the Cloud Services and related technical support,
                      excluding any Customer Data and Partner Data.</p>
                    <p>Service Data consists of:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <li><b>Account information. </b>We collect the data you or
                        your organization provide when creating an account for
                        Cloud Services or entering into a contract with us
                        (username, names, contact details and job titles).</li>
                      <li><strong>Cloud payments and
                          transactions.</strong>&nbsp;We keep reasonable
                        business records of charges, payments, and billing
                        details and issues.</li>
                      <li><strong>Cloud settings and configurations.</strong> We
                        record your configuration and settings, including
                        resource identifiers and attributes, and service and
                        security settings for data and other resources.</li>
                      <li><strong>Technical and operational details of your
                          usage of Cloud Services.</strong> We collect
                        information about usage, operational status, software
                        errors and crash reports, authentication details,
                        quality and performance metrics, and other technical
                        details necessary for us to operate and maintain Cloud
                        Services and related software. This information includes
                        device identifiers, identifiers from cookies or tokens,
                        and IP addresses.</li>
                      <li><strong>Your direct communications.</strong> We keep
                        records of your communications and interactions with us
                        and our partners (for example, when you provide
                        feedback, ask questions or seek technical support).</li>
                    </ul>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-2"
                  panel-title="Why We Process Service Data">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>Google processes Service Data for the following purposes:
                    </p>
                    <ul>
                      <li><strong>Provide Cloud Services you request.</strong>
                        We use Service Data primarily to deliver the Cloud
                        Services that you and our customers request. This
                        includes processing Service Data as needed to conduct
                        checks before extending credit to certain customers, to
                        bill for the Cloud Services used, to ensure those
                        services are delivered or working as intended, to detect
                        and avoid outages or other technical problems, and to
                        secure your data and services.</li>
                      <li><strong>Make recommendations to optimize use of Cloud
                          Services.</strong> We use Service Data to provide you
                        and our customers with recommendations (for example,
                        suggesting ways to better secure your account or data,
                        reduce service charges or improve performance, or
                        optimize your configurations), and providing information
                        about new or related products and features. We also
                        evaluate your responses to our recommendations and other
                        feedback (if you choose to provide it).</li>
                      <li><strong>Maintain and improve Cloud Services.</strong>
                        We evaluate Service Data to help us improve the
                        performance and functionality of Cloud Services. As we
                        improve Cloud Services for you, this will improve them
                        for our customers, and vice versa.</li>
                      <li><strong>Provide and improve other services you
                          request.</strong> We use Service Data to deliver and
                        improve other services that you and our customers
                        request, including Google or third-party services that
                        are enabled via the Cloud Services, administrative
                        consoles, application programming interfaces (APIs) or
                        command line interfaces (CLIs), or the&nbsp;Google
                        Workspace Marketplace.</li>
                      <li><strong>Assist you.</strong> We use Service Data to
                        provide technical support for Cloud Services that you
                        and our customers request, and to assess whether we have
                        met your needs. We also use Service Data to improve our
                        technical support, inform you and our customers about
                        updates to Cloud Services and send other notifications
                        relating to Cloud Services.</li>
                      <li><strong>Protect you, our users,&nbsp;<b>customers,</b>
                          the public, and Google.</strong> We use Service Data
                        to detect, prevent and respond to fraud, abuse, security
                        risks, and technical issues that could harm you, other
                        users, our customers, the public, or Google.&nbsp;This
                        helps make our services safer, more reliable, and more
                        secure.</li>
                      <li><strong>Comply with legal obligations.</strong> We use
                        Service Data to comply with our legal obligations (for
                        example, where we’re responding to legal process or an
                        enforceable governmental request, or meeting our
                        financial record-keeping obligations).</li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>To achieve these processing purposes, we use algorithms
                      to recognize patterns in Service Data, manual review of
                      Service Data (such as when you interact directly with our
                      billing or support teams), aggregation or anonymization of
                      Service Data to eliminate personal information, and
                      combination of Service Data with information from other
                      Google products and services. We also use Service Data for
                      internal reporting and analysis of applicable product and
                      business operations.</p>
                    <p>Please note, if your organization has entered into our
                      <a href="https://workspace.google.com/terms/service-data-addendum.html" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="google workspace for education service data addendum" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="workspace.google.com/terms/service-data-addendum.html">Google Workspace for Education Service Data Addendum</a>:
                    </p>
                    <ul>
                      <li>your organization will process Service Data collected
                        or generated from Google Workspace for Education, as a
                        controller, for purposes it is required to disclose to
                        you separately; and</li>
                      <li>Google’s processing purposes listed above will not
                        apply to you. The purposes that apply to you are
                        described in the
                        <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice-supplement" class="cws-link" track-name="supplemental google cloud privacy notice" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice-supplement">Supplemental Google Cloud Privacy Notice</a>.
                        Please visit that link to learn more.</li>
                    </ul>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-3"
                  panel-title="Where Service Data Is Stored">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>We maintain data centers around the world, and provide
                      Google Workspace (including Google Workspace for
                      Education) and Cloud Identity (when sold separately) from
                      <a href="https://www.google.com/about/datacenters/inside/locations/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="cws-link" track-name="these locations" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="www.google.com/about/datacenters/inside/locations/">these locations</a>,
                      and Google Cloud Platform from
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/about/locations" class="cws-link" track-name="these locations" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/about/locations">these locations</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p>Service Data may be processed on servers located outside
                      of the country where our users and customers are located
                      because Service Data is typically processed by centralized
                      or regionalized operations like billing, support, and
                      security.</p>
                    <p>Regardless of where Service Data is processed, we apply
                      the same protections described in this Privacy Notice.
                      When transferring Service Data outside of the European
                      Economic Area, the UK or Switzerland, we comply with
                      certain
                      <a href="https://policies.google.com/privacy/frameworks" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="cws-link" track-name="legal frameworks" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="policies.google.com/privacy/frameworks">legal frameworks</a>.
                    </p>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-4"
                  panel-title="How We Secure Service Data">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>We build Cloud Services with strong security features to
                      protect your data. The insights we gain from providing our
                      services help us detect and automatically block security
                      threats from ever reaching you.</p>
                    <p>We work hard to protect the Service Data we hold from
                      unauthorized access, alteration, disclosure,
                      or&nbsp;destruction, including by:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <li>Encrypting Service Data at rest and while in transit
                        between our facilities.</li>
                      <li>Regularly reviewing our Service Data collection,
                        storage, and processing practices, including our
                        physical security measures, to prevent unauthorized
                        access to our systems; and</li>
                      <li>Restricting access to Service Data to Google
                        employees, contractors, and agents who need it in order
                        to process Service Data for us. Anyone with this access
                        is subject to strict contractual confidentiality
                        obligations and may be disciplined or terminated if they
                        fail to meet these obligations.</li>
                    </ul>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-5"
                  panel-title="How We Share Service Data">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>We instruct our affiliates to process Service Data for
                      the purposes listed under
                      “<a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-2" class="cws-link" track-name="why we process service data" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Why We Process Service Data</a>”
                      above, in compliance with this Privacy Notice and
                      appropriate confidentiality and security measures.&nbsp;
                    </p>
                    <p>We do not share Service Data with companies,
                      organizations, or individuals outside of Google except in
                      the following cases:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <ul>
                        <li>When you procure third-party services</li>
                      </ul>
                    </ul>
                    <p style="padding-left: 80px;">We share Service Data outside
                      of Google when you or our customer choose(s) to procure a
                      third-party service through Google Cloud Platform, the
                      Google Cloud Platform Marketplace or the Google Workspace
                      Marketplace, or use a third-party application that
                      requests access to your Service Data.</p>
                    <ul>
                      <ul>
                        <li>With your consent</li>
                      </ul>
                    </ul>
                    <p style="padding-left: 80px;">We’ll share Service Data
                      outside of Google where we have obtained your consent.</p>
                    <ul>
                      <ul>
                        <li>With your administrators and authorized resellers
                        </li>
                      </ul>
                    </ul>
                    <p style="padding-left: 80px;">When you use Cloud Services,
                      your administrator and resellers authorized to manage your
                      or your organization’s account will have access to certain
                      Service Data. For example, they may be able to:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <ul>
                        <ul>
                          <li>View account and billing information, activity and
                            statistics</li>
                          <li>Change your account password</li>
                          <li>Suspend or terminate your account access</li>
                          <li>Access your account information in order to
                            satisfy applicable law, regulation, legal process,
                            or enforceable governmental request</li>
                          <li>Restrict your ability to delete or edit your
                            information or your privacy settings</li>
                        </ul>
                        <li>For external processing</li>
                      </ul>
                    </ul>
                    <p style="padding-left: 80px;">We do not sell your Service
                      Data to any third parties.</p>
                    <p style="padding-left: 80px;">We share Service Data with
                      trusted third party providers to process it for us as we
                      instruct them and in compliance with this Privacy Notice
                      and appropriate confidentiality and security measures. In
                      particular, we share Service Data with our third party
                      providers when you request technical support services (we
                      share the information you provide in the support ticket,
                      and those providers may communicate with you or your
                      administrator in that ticket, including providing updates
                      and closing the ticket) and professional services (we
                      share your contact details to enable communication and
                      collaboration).</p>
                    <ul>
                      <ul>
                        <li>For legal reasons</li>
                      </ul>
                    </ul>
                    <p style="padding-left: 80px;">We share Service Data outside
                      of Google when we have a good-faith belief that access to,
                      or disclosure that Service Data is reasonably necessary
                      to:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <ul>
                        <ul>
                          <li>Comply with applicable law, regulation, legal
                            process, or enforceable governmental request. We
                            share information about the number and type of
                            requests we receive from governments in
                            our&nbsp;<a href="https://transparencyreport.google.com/user-data/overview" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="cws-link" track-name="transparency report" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="transparencyreport.google.com/user-data/overview">Transparency Report</a>.
                          </li>
                          <li>Enforce applicable agreements, including
                            investigation of potential violations.</li>
                          <li>Detect, prevent, or otherwise address fraud,
                            security, or technical issues.</li>
                          <li>Protect against harm to the rights, property or
                            safety of Google, our customers, users, and the
                            public as required or permitted by law.</li>
                        </ul>
                      </ul>
                    </ul>
                    <p style="padding-left: 80px;">If Google is involved in a
                      reorganization, merger, acquisition, or sale of assets,
                      we’ll continue to ensure the confidentiality of Service
                      Data and give affected users notice before Service Data
                      becomes subject to a different privacy policy.</p>
                    <ul></ul>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-6"
                  panel-title="Access to Service Data">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>Your organization may allow you to access and export your
                      data in order to back it up or transfer it to a service
                      outside of Google. Some Google Cloud Services enable you
                      to directly access and download the data you have stored
                      in the services. As further described in our
                      <a href="https://services.google.com/fh/gumdrop/preview/misc/gsuite_dsr_customer_guide.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="cws-link" track-name="google workspace data subject requests guide" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="services.google.com/fh/gumdrop/preview/misc/gsuite_dsr_customer_guide.pdf">Google Workspace Data Subject Requests Guide</a>,
                      you or your organization may use various tools to access,
                      control, and export your data.</p>
                    <p>You and your organization’s administrator can access
                      several types of Service Data directly from Google Cloud,
                      including your account information, billing contact
                      information, payment and transaction information, as well
                      as product and communication settings and configurations.
                    </p>
                    <p>If you’re otherwise unable to access your Service Data,
                      you can always request it
                      <a href="https://support.google.com/policies/answer/9581826" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="support.google.com/policies/answer/9581826">here</a>.
                    </p>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-7"
                  panel-title="Retention and Deletion of Service Data">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>We retain Service Data for different periods of time
                      depending on the type of data, how we use it, and how you
                      configure your settings. When we no longer need Service
                      Data, we delete or anonymize it.</p>
                    <p>For each type of Service Data and processing operation,
                      we set retention timeframes based on the purposes for
                      which we process it, and ensure that the Service Data is
                      kept for no longer than necessary. We retain most types of
                      Service Data for a set period of up to 180 days (the exact
                      number depends on the specific type of data). However,
                      some Service Data may be kept for longer periods where
                      there is a business need. We generally have longer
                      retention periods (which can be over a year) for Service
                      Data that is kept for the following purposes:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <li><b>Security, fraud and abuse prevention. </b>We retain
                        Service Data when it is necessary to protect against
                        fraudulent attempts to gain access to user accounts, or
                        to investigate violations of applicable Cloud Services
                        agreements. Usually, the Service Data retained where
                        there is reason to suspect fraud or abuse would include
                        device identifiers, identifiers from cookies or tokens,
                        and IP addresses, as well as log data about usage of the
                        Cloud Services.&nbsp;</li>
                      <li>
                        <b>Complying with legal or regulatory requirements. </b>We
                        retain Service Data when required by an enforceable
                        legal process, such as when Google receives a lawful
                        subpoena.&nbsp;</li>
                      <li>
                        <b>Complying with tax, accounting or financial requirements.</b>
                        When Google processes a payment for you, or when you
                        make a payment to Google, we retain Service Data about
                        those transactions (including billing information),
                        typically for a minimum of five years, as required for
                        tax or accounting purposes, or to comply with applicable
                        financial regulations.</li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>At the end of the applicable retention period, we follow
                      detailed protocols to make sure that the Service Data is
                      securely and completely deleted from our active systems
                      (the servers Google uses to run applications and store
                      data) or retained only in anonymized form. After
                      completion of these steps, copies of Service Data will
                      remain for a limited period in our encrypted backup
                      systems (which we maintain to protect Service Data from
                      accidental or malicious deletion and for outage and
                      disaster recovery purposes), before being overwritten by
                      new backup copies.</p>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-8"
                  panel-title="Using Google Accounts and Products">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>Your Google Account is your connection to all Google
                      products and services, not just Cloud Services. When you
                      choose to use Google products and services outside of
                      Cloud Services,
                      the&nbsp;<a href="https://policies.google.com/privacy" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="cws-link" track-name="google privacy policy" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="policies.google.com/privacy">Google Privacy Policy</a>
                      describes how your personal information (including your
                      Google Account profile information) is collected and used.
                      You and your administrator can control which other Google
                      services you may use while logged into a Google Account
                      managed by your organization.</p>
                    <p>If you interact with Cloud Services using a Google
                      Account managed by your organization, then your personal
                      information may be subject to your organization’s privacy
                      policies and processes, and you should direct privacy
                      inquiries to your organization.</p>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-9"
                  panel-title="European Privacy Standards and GDPR">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p><b>Exercising your data protection rights</b></p>
                    <p>If European Union (EU), UK or Swiss data protection law
                      applies to the processing of Service Data relating to you,
                      you have certain rights, including the rights to access,
                      correct, delete and export your Service Data, and to
                      object to or request that we restrict processing of your
                      Service Data.</p>
                    <p>Google Cloud EMEA Ltd will be the data controller
                      responsible for your Service Data. However, where our
                      customer has entered into an agreement covering Cloud
                      Services with a different Google affiliate, that affiliate
                      will be the data controller responsible for processing
                      your Service Data in connection with billing for the Cloud
                      Services only.</p>
                    <p>If you want to exercise your data protection rights with
                      regard to Service Data we process in accordance with this
                      Privacy Notice, and you are not able to do so via the
                      tools available to you or your organization’s
                      administrator, you can contact Google via our
                      <a href="https://support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="privacy help center" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/">Privacy Help Center</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p>You can always contact your local data protection
                      authority if you have concerns regarding your rights under
                      local law.</p>
                    <p><b>Our grounds for processing your Service Data</b></p>
                    <p>When we process Service Data for the purposes described
                      in this Privacy Notice (see "Why We Process Service Data”
                      above), we rely on the following legal grounds:</p>

                                third parties’ <b>legitimate interests</b> to
                                protect against harm to our users, our customers
                                and the public, including criminal acts and
                                rights violations.</p>
                            </td>
                          </tr>
                          <tr>
                            <td>
                              <p>Comply with legal obligations.&nbsp;</p>
                            </td>
                            <td>
                              <p>Depending on the specific legal obligations,
                                the following types of Service Data:</p>
                              <ul>
                                <li>Account information</li>
                                <li>Cloud payments and transactions</li>
                                <li>Cloud settings and configurations</li>
                                <li>Technical and operational details of your
                                  use of Cloud Services</li>
                                <li>Your direct communications</li>
                              </ul>
                            </td>
                            <td>
                              <p>When we have a <b>legal obligation</b> to do
                                so. For example, where we’re responding to legal
                                process or an enforceable governmental request,
                                or retaining information relating to your
                                purchases and communications to meet our
                                record-keeping obligations.</p>
                            </td>
                          </tr>
                        </tbody>
                      </table>
                    </div>

                      <a href="https://workspace.google.com/terms/service-data-addendum.html" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="google workspace for education service data addendum" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="workspace.google.com/terms/service-data-addendum.html">Google Workspace for Education Service Data Addendum</a>,

                      for information about the legal grounds we rely on when

                      Stored’ (above) for information on where we and our

                      country in the world.</p>

                      transfer of information as set out in our
                      <a href="https://policies.google.com/privacy/frameworks" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="legal frameworks for data transfers" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="policies.google.com/privacy/frameworks">Legal Frameworks for Data Transfers</a>
                      page. We may also transfer your information to a third
                      country based on an exception provided for by the Swiss
                      Federal Data Protection Act.</p>
                    <p>An exception may apply in the event of legal proceedings
                      abroad, in cases of overriding public interest or if the
                      performance of a contract with you or in your interest
                      requires disclosure, if you have consented, if the
                      information has been made generally available by you and
                      you have not objected to the processing, or the disclosure
                      is necessary in order to protect the life or the physical
                      integrity of you or a third party and we can't get consent
                      within a reasonable period of time, or the information
                      originates from a register provided for by Swiss law which
                      is accessible to the public or to persons with a
                      legitimate interest, provided that the legal conditions
                      for the consultation of such register has been met in the
                      specific case.</p>

                    <p>If Brazilian data protection law applies to the
                      processing of Service Data, you have certain rights,
                      including the rights to access, correct, delete or export
                      your Service Data, as well as to object to or request that
                      we restrict processing of Service Data. You also have the
                      right to object to the processing of Service Data or to
                      export Service Data to another service.</p>
                    <p>For users based in Brazil, the data controller
                      responsible for Service Data we collect for Google
                      Workspace and Google Workspace for Education is Google
                      LLC, and the data controller responsible for Service Data
                      we collect for Google Cloud Platform is Cloud Brasil
                      Computação e Serviços de Dados Ltda. If you want to
                      exercise your data protection rights with regard to
                      Service Data we process in accordance with this Privacy
                      Notice and are not able to do so via the tools available
                      to you or your organization’s administrator, you can
                      always contact Google via our
                      <a href="https://support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="cws-link" track-name="privacy help center" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/">Privacy Help Center</a>.
                      And you can contact your data protection authority if you
                      have concerns regarding your rights under Brazilian law.
                    </p>
                    <p>In addition to the purposes and grounds described in this
                      Privacy Notice, we may process Service Data on the
                      following legal grounds:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <li><strong>Where necessary for the performance of a
                          contract with you</strong>
                        <p>We may process your information where necessary for
                          us to enter into a contract with you or to comply with
                          our contractual commitments to you.</p>
                      </li>
                      <li><strong>When we’re complying with legal
                          obligations</strong>
                        <p>We’ll process your information when we have a legal
                          obligation to do so.</p>
                      </li>
                      <li><strong>When we’re pursuing legitimate
                          interests</strong>
                        <p>We may process Service Data based on our legitimate
                          interests and those of third parties while applying
                          appropriate safeguards that protect your privacy. This
                          means that we process your information in the
                          interests of providing Cloud Services you request;
                          making recommendations to optimize use of Cloud
                          Services; maintaining and improving Cloud Services;
                          providing and improving other services you request;
                          assisting you; and protecting against harm to the
                          rights, property or safety of Google, our users, our
                          customers, and the public, as required or permitted by
                          law.</p>
                      </li>
                    </ul>

                    <p>Some U.S. state privacy laws require specific
                      disclosures.</p>
                    <p>These laws may include</p>
                    <ul>
                      <li>California Consumer Privacy Act (CCPA);</li>
                      <li>Virginia Consumer Data Protection Act (VCDPA);</li>
                      <li>Colorado Privacy Act (CPA);</li>
                      <li>Connecticut Act Concerning Personal Data Privacy and
                        Online Monitoring (CTDPA); and</li>
                      <li>Utah Consumer Privacy Act (UCPA)</li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>This Privacy Notice is designed to help you understand
                      how Google handles Service Data:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <li>
                        <p>We explain the categories of Service Data Google
                          collects and the sources of that Service Data in
                          <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-1" class="cws-link" track-name="service data we collect" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Service Data We Collect</a>.
                        </p>
                      </li>
                      <li>
                        <p>We explain the purposes for which Google collects and
                          uses Service Data in
                          <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-2" class="cws-link" track-name="why we process service data" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Why We Process Service Data</a>.
                        </p>
                      </li>
                      <li>
                        <p>We explain when Google may disclose Service Data in
                          <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-5" class="cws-link" track-name="how we share service data" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">How We Share Service Data</a>.
                          Google does not sell your Service Data to any third
                          parties. Google also does not “share” your Service
                          Data as that term is defined in the California
                          Consumer Privacy Act (CCPA).</p>
                      </li>
                      <li>
                        <p>We explain how Google retains Service Data in
                          <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-7" class="cws-link" track-name="retention and deletion of service data" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Retention and Deletion of Service Data</a>.
                          We maintain policies and technical measures to avoid
                          re-identifying that information.</p>
                      </li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>U.S. state privacy laws also provide the right to request
                      information about how Google collects, uses, and discloses
                      Service Data. And they give you the right to access your
                      Service Data, sometimes in a portable format;&nbsp;
                      correct Service Data; and to request that Google delete
                      that Service Data. They also provide the right to not be
                      discriminated against for exercising these privacy rights.
                    </p>
                    <p>We provide the information and tools described in
                      <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-6" class="cws-link" track-name="access to service data" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Access to Service Data</a>
                      so you can exercise these rights. When you use them, we’ll
                      validate your request by verifying your identity (for
                      example, by confirming that you’re signed in to your
                      Google Account).</p>
                    <p>If you have questions or requests related to your rights
                      under U.S. state privacy laws, you (or your authorized
                      agent) can also
                      <a href="https://support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="contact google" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/">contact Google</a>.
                      And if you disagree with the decision on your request, you

                      email.</p>

                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>If Korean data protection law applies to the processing
                      of your Service Data, we provide the following additional
                      information for users of Cloud Services residing in Korea.
                    </p>
                    <p><b>Items of personal information collected.</b> When you
                      use our Cloud Services, the following Service Data is
                      collected: (i) data you provide when creating an account
                      for Cloud Services or entering into a contract with us
                      (credentials, names, contact details, job titles, date of
                      birth and gender), (ii) business records of charges,
                      payments, billing details and issues; credit card info and
                      connecting info (iii) configuration and settings,
                      including resource identifiers and attributes, and service
                      and security settings, (iv) usage, operational status,
                      software errors and crash reports, authentication
                      credentials, quality and performance metrics, and other
                      technical details, device identifiers, identifiers from
                      cookies or tokens, and IP addresses), (v) your
                      communications and interactions with us and our partners,
                      and feedback, each as further described
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#0" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p>The personal information listed in (i) to (v) above may
                      be transmitted to our
                      <a href="https://www.google.com/about/datacenters/locations/" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="data centers" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="www.google.com/about/datacenters/locations/">data centers</a>
                      located abroad through our network, as described in
                      Purposes of collection and use of personal information
                      below and stored for the retention period described in
                      Retention period and deletion of personal information
                      below. If you do not want your personal information to be
                      transferred overseas, you may refrain from using services
                      and not provide your personal information. However,
                      services may not be provided or may be limited. If you
                      have any questions about this, please see the Contact
                      Information below.</p>
                    <p>We may use cookies (small text files placed on the user's
                      device) and similar technologies for a variety of
                      purposes, including user preferences or settings,
                      authentication information, or analysis. Most web browsers
                      accept cookies automatically, but provide controls that
                      allow you to block or delete cookies.</p>
                    <p>
                      <b>Purpose of collection and use of personal information.</b>
                      Google collects and uses Service Data (i) to provide Cloud
                      Services you request, (ii) to make recommendations to
                      optimize use of Cloud Services, (iii) to maintain and
                      improve Cloud Services, (iv) to provide and improve other
                      services you request (v) to assist you, (vi) to protect
                      you, our users, customers, the public and Google, and
                      (vii) to comply with legal obligations, each as further
                      described
                      <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-2" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p><strong>Retention period&nbsp;<b>and deletion</b> of
                        <b>personal information.</b></strong>&nbsp;Service Data
                      is deleted or anonymized once it is no longer needed for
                      the purposes described above. For each type of data and
                      operation, we set retention timeframes based on the
                      purpose for its collection, and ensure it is kept for no
                      longer than necessary.</p>
                    <p>If the retention period expires or you request deletion,
                      Google will faithfully endeavor to delete such Service
                      Data unless there is a legal obligation that requires
                      processing or another lawful basis for retaining the
                      Service Data. When we receive a request to delete Service
                      Data, the retention period of the archive copy expires,
                      and then Google's archiving system has a mechanism to
                      overwrite the expired data.</p>
                    <p>We retain most types of Service Data for a set period of
                      up to 180 days (the exact number depends on the specific
                      type of data).&nbsp; However, we generally have longer
                      retention periods (which can be over a year) for Service
                      Data that is kept for (i) Security, fraud and abuse
                      prevention, (ii) complying with legal or regulatory
                      requirements including the Communications Secrets
                      Protection Act. We also have retention periods of a
                      minimum of five years for Service Data about payments and
                      billing information for&nbsp; complying with tax,
                      accounting or financial requirements, each as further
                      described
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-7" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p><b>Consignment of personal information processing.</b> We
                      provide information to affiliates (listed
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/subprocessors" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/subprocessors">here</a>
                      for Google Cloud Platform, and
                      <a href="https://workspace.google.com/intl/en/terms/subprocessors.html" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="workspace.google.com/intl/en/terms/subprocessors.html">here</a>
                      for Google Workspace and Google Workspace for Education),
                      partners and other trusted businesses or persons to
                      process it for us, based on our instructions and in
                      compliance with this Privacy Notice and other appropriate
                      confidentiality and security measures.</p>
                    <p>Google has contracts with the third-party service
                      providers listed below to provide Cloud Services to Korean
                      residents. The contracts impose obligations on those
                      companies to prohibit the processing of Service Data other
                      than for the purposes we specify, to return or destroy
                      Service Data after the end of processing, and to implement
                      processes to ensure those companies comply with these
                      obligations. &nbsp;</p>

                      questions about the Google Cloud Privacy Notice or privacy
                      practices, please contact our Google privacy team (Email:
                      <a href="mailto:googlekrsupport@google.com" class="cws-link" track-name="googlekrsupportgooglecom" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="mailto:googlekrsupport@google.com">googlekrsupport@google.com</a>).
                    </p>
                    <p></p>
                    <p>If you want to exercise your data protection rights with
                      regard to Service Data we process in accordance with this
                      Privacy Notice and are not able to do so via the tools
                      available to you or your organization’s administrator, you
                      can always contact Google via our
                      <a href="https://support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="privacy help center" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="support.google.com/policies/troubleshooter/7575787/">Privacy Help Center</a>.
                      And you can contact your local data protection authority
                      (<i>for instance, </i><a href="http://privacy.kisa.or.kr" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="personal information infringement report center" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="privacy.kisa.or.kr"><i>Personal Information Infringement Report Center</i></a>)
                      if you have concerns regarding your rights under Korean
                      privacy law.</p>
                    <p>For local representatives under Personal Information
                      Protection Act and the Act on Promotion of Information and
                      Communication Network Utilization and Information
                      Protection, please see below:</p>
                    <ul>
                      <li>Name and Representative: D-Agent Co., Ltd. (CEO
                        &nbsp;Byung-gun An)</li>
                      <li>Address and Contact Information: #1116, Platinum
                        Building, Gwanghwamun 28, Saemunan-ro 5-ga-gil,
                        Jongno-gu, Seoul, 02-737-0346, google_da_kr@dagent.co.kr
                      </li>
                    </ul>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-13"
                  panel-title="Japan Requirements">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>If Japanese data protection law (the Act on the
                      Protection of Personal Information, “APPI”) applies to the
                      processing of your Service Data, we provide the following
                      additional information for users of Cloud Services
                      residing in Japan.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
                    <p><b>Controller of Service Data.&nbsp; </b>Any Service Data
                      provided to or gathered by Google is controlled primarily
                      by Google LLC, located at 1600 Amphitheatre Parkway
                      Mountain View, CA 94043 United States, representative is
                      Sundar Pichai, CEO.</p>
                    <p>
                      <b>Purpose of collection and use of personal information.</b>
                      Google collects and uses Services Data for the purposes
                      set out
                      <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-1" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>
                      and
                      <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-2" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p>
                      <b>Measures undertaken to protect retained personal information.&nbsp;</b>
                    </p>
                    <p><b><i>Establishment of general policy</i></b></p>
                    <p>Google establishes and publishes this
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice" class="cws-link" track-name="privacy notice" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Privacy Notice</a>
                      outlining our general policy relating to Service Data.</p>
                    <p>
                      <b><i>Establishment of internal policy relating to handling of personal data</i></b>
                    </p>
                    <p>Google establishes internal policies about handling
                      measures and persons in charge and their responsibility
                      etc. with regard to the acquisition, utilization, records,
                      provision, deletion etc. of personal data.</p>
                    <p>
                      <b><i>Internal organization as security control action</i></b>
                    </p>
                    <p>Google has large security and privacy teams responsible
                      for developing, implementing, and reviewing internal
                      personal data handling processes. Google employees are
                      trained to report suspected incidents involving personal
                      data, which may be done through various channels such as
                      through dedicated email addresses or digital platforms. A
                      dedicated team assesses reported incidents, and as
                      appropriate a coordinated team is assigned to manage the
                      overall incident, including liaising with Legal and the
                      product team as part of the investigation and response.
                      The team on-call for an incident is assigned on a daily
                      rotation. Incident responses may follow either a standard
                      or an expedited route, depending on the severity and
                      priority assigned to the incident.</p>
                    <p>
                      <b><i>Personnel measures as security control action</i></b>
                    </p>
                    <p>Google conducts periodical training for its employees
                      about matters to consider when handling personal data.</p>
                    <p>
                      <b><i>Physical measures as security control action</i></b>
                    </p>
                    <p>Google takes measures to prevent unauthorized persons
                      from accessing personal data in any situation and to
                      prevent theft or loss of devices and electronic media for
                      handling personal data.</p>
                    <p>
                      <b><i>Technical measures as security control action</i></b>
                    </p>
                    <p>Please see
                      <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-4" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>
                      and
                      <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-7" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>
                      for further information on the security measures
                      undertaken to secure, retain and delete Service
                      Data<b>.&nbsp;&nbsp;</b></p>
                    <p><b><i>Research of external environment</i></b></p>
                    <p>Data protection laws vary among countries, with some
                      providing more protection than others. Google has
                      established a personal information protection system to
                      ensure your information is accorded protections equivalent
                      to APPI, as described in the
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice" class="cws-link" track-name="privacy notice" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Privacy Notice</a>.
                      Regardless of where your information is processed, Google
                      applies the same&nbsp; personal information protection
                      measures globally. We also comply with certain legal
                      frameworks relating to the transfer of data, such as the
                      European frameworks. For more detail, please see
                      <a href="https://policies.google.com/privacy/frameworks" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="data transfer frameworks" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="policies.google.com/privacy/frameworks">Data transfer frameworks</a>.
                      Further, with regard to the location of our data centers
                      storing Service Data, please see
                      <a href="/terms/cloud-privacy-notice#panel0-3" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">here</a>.
                      There may be cases where Google entrusts the processing of
                      information to subprocessors or its subsidiaries or
                      affiliates. With regard to the location of Google’s
                      offices including subsidiaries and affiliates, please see
                      <a href="https://about.google/locations/?region=asia-pacific&amp;office=tokyo-rpg" class="cws-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener" track-name="googles office locations" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="about.google/locations/">Google’s Office Locations</a>.
                      With regard to the location of subprocessors, please see
                      <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/subprocessors" class="cws-link" track-name="here" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="cloud.google.com/terms/subprocessors">here</a>.
                    </p>
                    <p><b>Contact information.&nbsp; </b>For any inquiries or
                      requests about your Service Data related rights under
                      applicable law, please email
                      <a href="mailto:appi-inquiries-external@google.com" class="cws-link" track-name="appi-inquiries-externalgooglecom" track-type="inline link" track-metadata-eventdetail="mailto:appi-inquiries-external@google.com">appi-inquiries-external@google.com</a>.
                    </p>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
                <cws-accordion-panel slot="panel" id="panel0-14"
                  panel-title="Updates to this Privacy Notice">
                  <span class="cws-body richtext">
                    <p>We may update this Privacy Notice from time to time. We
                      will not make any significant changes without notifying
                      you in advance by posting a prominent notice on this page
                      describing the changes or by sending you a direct
                      communication. We encourage you to regularly review this
                      Privacy Notice, and we will always indicate the date the
                      last changes were published.</p>
                  </span>
                </cws-accordion-panel>
              </cws-accordion>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
